# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="4460b-102">Veraltete Typen in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="4460b-103"><a name="introduction"></a> In den Tabellen dieses Artikels sind die Typen aufgeführt, die in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] und [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] veraltet sind, geordnet nach Assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-103"><a name="introduction"></a> The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4460b-104">Über die nachfolgenden Links finden Sie eine Liste der veralteten Typen und empfohlenen Alternativen in den jeweiligen Assemblys.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4460b-105">Da diese Typen veraltet sind, sind alle ihrer Member ebenfalls veraltet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4460b-106">Eine Liste weiterer veralteter Member in der .NET Framework-Klassenbibliothek finden Sie unter [Veraltete Member](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="4460b-133">Veraltete Typen in Systemassemblys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="4460b-134">In den folgenden Tabellen sind die Typen aufgeführt, die in Systemassemblys als veraltet eingestuft wurden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4460b-135">Diese Assemblys werden zur allgemeinen Anwendungsentwicklung für .NET Framework verwendet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="4460b-925">Veraltete Typen in Microsoft-Assemblys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-925">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="4460b-926">In den folgenden Abschnitten sind die veralteten Typen in Microsoft-Assemblys aufgeführt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-926">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4460b-927">Bei diesen Assemblys handelt es sich um zweckgebundene Assemblys, beispielsweise Assemblys, die auf eine einzelne Sprache abzielen (z. B. Microsoft.JScript.dll oder Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4460b-927">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>
